         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # --- Helper functions to read/write pipe-delimited files ---
         
         def read_vehicles() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             vehicles = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'vehicles.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 9:
                             continue
                         vehicle = {
                             'vehicle_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'make': parts[1],
                             'model': parts[2],
                             'vehicle_type': parts[3],
                             'daily_rate': float(parts[4]),
                             'seats': int(parts[5]),
                             'transmission': parts[6],
                             'fuel_type': parts[7],
                             'status': parts[8]
                         }
                         vehicles.append(vehicle)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return vehicles
         
         
         def read_customers() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             customers = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'customers.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         customer = {
                             'customer_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'name': parts[1],
                             'email': parts[2],
                             'phone': parts[3],
                             'driver_license': parts[4],
                             'license_expiry': parts[5]
                         }
                         customers.append(customer)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return customers

         def read_rentals() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             rentals = []

         def write_rentals(rentals: List[Dict[str, Any]]):
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'rentals.txt'), 'w') as f:
                     for rental in rentals:
                         line = f"{rental['rental_id']}|{rental['vehicle_id']}|{rental['customer_id']}|{rental['pickup_date']}|{rental['dropoff_date']}|{rental['pickup_location']}|{rental['dropoff_location']}|{rental['total_price']}|{rental['status']}\n"
                         f.write(line)
             except Exception:

         def read_insurance() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             insurances = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'insurance.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         # coverage_limit may be str or int
                         try:
                             coverage_limit = int(parts[4])
                         except ValueError:
                             coverage_limit = parts[4]
                         insurance = {
                             'insurance_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'plan_name': parts[1],
                             'description': parts[2],

                             'coverage_limit': coverage_limit,
                             'deductible': int(parts[5])
                         }
                         insurances.append(insurance)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return insurances
         
         
         def read_reservations() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:

         def write_reservations(reservations: List[Dict[str, Any]]):
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reservations.txt'), 'w') as f:
                     for r in reservations:
                         line = f"{r['reservation_id']}|{r['rental_id']}|{r['vehicle_id']}|{r['customer_id']}|{r['status']}|{r['insurance_id']}|{r['special_requests']}\n"

             except Exception:
                 pass
         
         # --- Utility functions ---
         
         def get_next_reservation_id() -> int:
             reservations = read_reservations()
             if reservations:
                 return max(r['reservation_id'] for r in reservations) + 1
             else:
                 return 1
         
         def get_next_rental_id() -> int:
             rentals = read_rentals()
             if rentals:
                 return max(r['rental_id'] for r in rentals) + 1
             else:
                 return 1
         
         # --- Routes Implementation ---
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             # Redirect to /dashboard as mandatory
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             # featured_vehicles: List[Dict[str, Any]] (vehicles), promotions: List[str]
             vehicles = read_vehicles()
             # Let's assume featured vehicles are first 5 available vehicles
             featured_vehicles = [v for v in vehicles if v['status'] == 'Available'][:5]
             
             promotions = [
                 "Weekend Special: 20% off SUVs",
                 "Free GPS with bookings over 3 days",
                 "Early Bird Discount: 15% off on weekday rentals"
             ]
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_vehicles=featured_vehicles, promotions=promotions)
         
         
         @app.route('/search-vehicles')
         def search_vehicles():
             # locations: List[str], vehicle_types: List[str], vehicles: List[Dict[str, Any]]
             locations_data = read_locations()
             locations = sorted({loc['city'] for loc in locations_data})
             vehicle_types = ['Economy', 'Compact', 'Sedan', 'SUV', 'Luxury']
             vehicles = read_vehicles()
             return render_template('search_vehicles.html', locations=locations, vehicle_types=vehicle_types, vehicles=vehicles)
         
         
         @app.route('/vehicle/<int:vehicle_id>')
         def vehicle_details(vehicle_id: int):
             vehicles = read_vehicles()
             vehicle = next((v for v in vehicles if v['vehicle_id'] == vehicle_id), None)
             if vehicle is None:
                 return "Vehicle not found", 404
             # There is no reviews.txt specified, reviews should be an empty list as no data source given
             reviews: List[Dict[str, Union[str, int, float]]] = []
             return render_template('vehicle_details.html', vehicle=vehicle, reviews=reviews)
         
         
         @app.route('/book/<int:vehicle_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def booking(vehicle_id: int):
             vehicles = read_vehicles()
             vehicle = next((v for v in vehicles if v['vehicle_id'] == vehicle_id), None)
             if vehicle is None or vehicle['status'] != 'Available':
                 return "Vehicle not available for booking", 400
         
             locations = read_locations()
             pickup_locations = [loc['city'] for loc in locations]
             dropoff_locations = pickup_locations.copy()
             booking_form: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None
             total_price: Optional[float] = None
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 pickup_location = request.form.get('pickup_location', '').strip()
                 dropoff_location = request.form.get('dropoff_location', '').strip()
                 pickup_date = request.form.get('pickup_date', '').strip()
                 dropoff_date = request.form.get('dropoff_date', '').strip()
         
                 # Validate pickup and dropoff locations
                 if pickup_location not in pickup_locations or dropoff_location not in dropoff_locations:
                     return "Invalid pickup or dropoff location", 400
         
                 # Validate dates format and logic
                 try:
                     pickup_dt = datetime.datetime.strptime(pickup_date, '%Y-%m-%d').date()
                     dropoff_dt = datetime.datetime.strptime(dropoff_date, '%Y-%m-%d').date()
                     if dropoff_dt < pickup_dt:
                         return "Dropoff date cannot be before pickup date", 400
                 except Exception:
                     return "Invalid date format", 400
         
                 # Calculate total price
                 days = (dropoff_dt - pickup_dt).days + 1
                 total_price = round(days * vehicle['daily_rate'], 2)
         
                 booking_form = {
                     'pickup_location': pickup_location,
                     'dropoff_location': dropoff_location,
                     'pickup_date': pickup_date,
                     'dropoff_date': dropoff_date
                 }
         
             return render_template('booking.html',
                                    pickup_locations=pickup_locations,
                                    dropoff_locations=dropoff_locations,
                                    booking_form=booking_form,
                                    total_price=total_price)
         
         
         @app.route('/insurance/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def insurance_options(reservation_id: int):
             insurance_plans = read_insurance()
             selected_insurance_id: Optional[int] = None
             insurance_details: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
         
             # Find reservation to ensure it exists
             reservations = read_reservations()
             reservation = next((r for r in reservations if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id), None)
             if reservation is None:
                 return "Reservation not found", 404
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 try:
                     selected_insurance_id = int(request.form.get('insurance_id', ''))
                 except (TypeError, ValueError):
                     return "Invalid insurance selection", 400
         
                 # Validate selected insurance id exists
                 insurance_details = next((i for i in insurance_plans if i['insurance_id'] == selected_insurance_id), None)
                 if insurance_details is None:
                     return "Selected insurance plan not found", 400
         
                 # Update reservation insurance_id
                 for r in reservations:
                     if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id:
                         r['insurance_id'] = selected_insurance_id
                         # Update reservation status to Confirmed as insurance selected
                         r['status'] = 'Confirmed'
                         break
                 write_reservations(reservations)
         
                 # Redirect or show confirmation - let's redirect to rental history
                 return redirect(url_for('rental_history'))
         
             # GET request
             if reservation['insurance_id'] != 0:
                 selected_insurance_id = reservation['insurance_id']
                 insurance_details = next((i for i in insurance_plans if i['insurance_id'] == selected_insurance_id), None)
             return render_template('insurance_options.html',
                                    insurance_plans=insurance_plans,
                                    selected_insurance_id=selected_insurance_id,
                                    insurance_details=insurance_details)
         
         
         @app.route('/rental-history')
         def rental_history():
             # rentals: List[Dict[str, Any]], status_filter_options: List[str], applied_status_filter: str
             rentals = read_rentals()
             # Get status filter from query string or default 'All'
             status_filter_options = ['All', 'Active', 'Completed', 'Cancelled']
             applied_status_filter = request.args.get('status_filter', 'All')
         
             if applied_status_filter != 'All':
                 rentals = [r for r in rentals if r['status'] == applied_status_filter]
         
             return render_template('rental_history.html',
                                    rentals=rentals,
                                    status_filter_options=status_filter_options,
                                    applied_status_filter=applied_status_filter)
         
         
         @app.route('/my-reservations')
         def reservations_page():
             reservations = read_reservations()
             return render_template('reservations.html', reservations=reservations)
         
         
         @app.route('/modify-reservation/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def modify_reservation(reservation_id:int):
             # Load reservation
             reservations = read_reservations()
             reservation = next((r for r in reservations if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id), None)
             if reservation is None:
                 return "Reservation not found", 404
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # No schema for modifications given, so cannot update fields
                 # But for implementation, we return error if trying to POST without details
                 # We do not have fields to modify as per spec, so just redirect back
                 return redirect(url_for('reservations_page'))
         
             # For GET return reservation
             return render_template('modify_reservation.html', reservation=reservation)
         
         
         @app.route('/cancel-reservation/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def cancel_reservation(reservation_id: int):
             reservations = read_reservations()
             found = False
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id:
                     r['status'] = 'Cancelled'
                     found = True
                     break
             if found:
                 write_reservations(reservations)
                 # Redirect back to reservations page
                 return redirect(url_for('reservations_page'))
             return "Reservation not found", 404
         
         
         @app.route('/special-requests', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def special_requests():
             reservations = read_reservations()
             submitted_data: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # form fields (by IDs in spec): select-reservation, driver-assistance-checkbox, gps-option-checkbox, child-seat-quantity, special-notes
                 try:
                     selected_reservation_id = int(request.form.get('select-reservation', '0'))
                 except ValueError:
                     return "Invalid reservation selection", 400
         
                 driver_assistance = 'driver-assistance-checkbox' in request.form
                 gps_option = 'gps-option-checkbox' in request.form
                 try:
                     child_seat_quantity = int(request.form.get('child-seat-quantity', '0'))
                     if child_seat_quantity < 0:
                         child_seat_quantity = 0
                 except ValueError:
                     child_seat_quantity = 0
                 special_notes = request.form.get('special-notes', '').strip()
         
                 # Append special requests to reservation special_requests (concatenate strings?)
                 reservations_data = []
                 for r in reservations:
                     if r['reservation_id'] == selected_reservation_id:
                         details = []
                         if driver_assistance:
                             details.append('Driver assistance requested')
                         if gps_option:
                             details.append('GPS option requested')
                         if child_seat_quantity > 0:
                             details.append(f'Child seats: {child_seat_quantity}')
                         if special_notes:
                             details.append(f'Notes: {special_notes}')
         
                         special_string = '; '.join(details) if details else ''
                         r['special_requests'] = special_string
                         submitted_data = {
                             'reservation_id': selected_reservation_id,
                             'driver_assistance': driver_assistance,
                             'gps_option': gps_option,
                             'child_seat_quantity': child_seat_quantity,
                             'special_notes': special_notes
                         }
                     reservations_data.append(r)
         
                 write_reservations(reservations_data)
         
             return render_template('special_requests.html', reservations=reservations, submitted_data=submitted_data)
         
         
         @app.route('/locations')
         def locations_page():
             locations = read_locations()
             hours_filter_options = ['24/7', 'Business Hours', 'Weekend']
             applied_hours_filter = request.args.get('hours_filter', '24/7')
             search_query = request.args.get('search_query', '').strip().lower()
         
             filtered_locations = locations
         
             # Apply hours filter
             if applied_hours_filter != '24/7':
                 if applied_hours_filter == 'Business Hours':
                     # Filter locations with hours matching 09:00-18:00 exactly
                     filtered_locations = [loc for loc in filtered_locations if loc['hours'] == '09:00-18:00']
                 elif applied_hours_filter == 'Weekend':
                     # No clear spec for weekend filter; no special marker in data, so no filter or empty
                     filtered_locations = []
         
             # Apply search query by city or name
             if search_query:
                 filtered_locations = [loc for loc in filtered_locations if search_query in loc['city'].lower() or search_query in loc['address'].lower()]
         
             return render_template('locations.html',
                                    locations=filtered_locations,
                                    hours_filter_options=hours_filter_options,
                                    applied_hours_filter=applied_hours_filter,
                                    search_query=search_query)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for
         from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional, Union
         import os
         import datetime
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # Helper functions to read data files
         
         def read_vehicles() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             vehicles = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'vehicles.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 9:
                             continue
                         vehicle = {
                             'vehicle_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'make': parts[1],
                             'model': parts[2],
                             'vehicle_type': parts[3],
                             'daily_rate': float(parts[4]),
                             'seats': int(parts[5]),
                             'transmission': parts[6],
                             'fuel_type': parts[7],
                             'status': parts[8]
                         }
                         vehicles.append(vehicle)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return vehicles
         
         
         def read_customers() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             customers = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'customers.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         customer = {
                             'customer_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'name': parts[1],
                             'email': parts[2],
                             'phone': parts[3],
                             'driver_license': parts[4],
                             'license_expiry': parts[5]
                         }
                         customers.append(customer)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return customers
         
         
         def read_locations() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             locations = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'locations.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         location = {
                             'location_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'city': parts[1],
                             'address': parts[2],
                             'phone': parts[3],
                             'hours': parts[4],
                             'available_vehicles': int(parts[5])
                         }
                         locations.append(location)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return locations
         
         
         def read_rentals() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             rentals = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'rentals.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 9:
                             continue
                         rental = {
                             'rental_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'vehicle_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'customer_id': int(parts[2]),
                             'pickup_date': parts[3],
                             'dropoff_date': parts[4],
                             'pickup_location': parts[5],
                             'dropoff_location': parts[6],
                             'total_price': float(parts[7]),
                             'status': parts[8]
                         }
                         rentals.append(rental)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return rentals
         
         
         def write_rentals(rentals: List[Dict[str, Any]]):
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'rentals.txt'), 'w') as f:
                     for rental in rentals:
                         line = f"{rental['rental_id']}|{rental['vehicle_id']}|{rental['customer_id']}|{rental['pickup_date']}|{rental['dropoff_date']}|{rental['pickup_location']}|{rental['dropoff_location']}|{rental['total_price']}|{rental['status']}\n"
                         f.write(line)
             except Exception:
                 pass
         
         
         def read_insurance() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             insurances = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'insurance.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         try:
                             coverage_limit = int(parts[4])
                         except ValueError:
                             coverage_limit = parts[4]
                         insurance = {
                             'insurance_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'plan_name': parts[1],
                             'description': parts[2],
                             'daily_cost': float(parts[3]),
                             'coverage_limit': coverage_limit,
                             'deductible': int(parts[5])
                         }
                         insurances.append(insurance)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return insurances
         
         
         def read_reservations() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             reservations = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reservations.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         reservation = {
                             'reservation_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'rental_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'vehicle_id': int(parts[2]),
                             'customer_id': int(parts[3]),
                             'status': parts[4],
                             'insurance_id': int(parts[5]),
                             'special_requests': parts[6]
                         }
                         reservations.append(reservation)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return reservations
         
         
         def write_reservations(reservations: List[Dict[str, Any]]):
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reservations.txt'), 'w') as f:
                     for r in reservations:
                         line = f"{r['reservation_id']}|{r['rental_id']}|{r['vehicle_id']}|{r['customer_id']}|{r['status']}|{r['insurance_id']}|{r['special_requests']}\n"
                         f.write(line)
             except Exception:
                 pass
         
         # Utility functions for auto id
         
         def get_next_reservation_id() -> int:
             reservations = read_reservations()
             return max([r['reservation_id'] for r in reservations], default=0) + 1
         
         def get_next_rental_id() -> int:
             rentals = read_rentals()
             return max([r['rental_id'] for r in rentals], default=0) + 1
         
         
         # ===================== ROUTES =====================
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             vehicles = read_vehicles()
             featured_vehicles = [v for v in vehicles if v['status'] == 'Available'][:5]
             promotions = [
                 "Weekend Special: 20% off SUVs",
                 "Free GPS with bookings over 3 days",
                 "Early Bird Discount: 15% off on weekday rentals"
             ]
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_vehicles=featured_vehicles, promotions=promotions)
         
         
         @app.route('/search-vehicles')
         def search_vehicles():
             locations_data = read_locations()
             locations = sorted({loc['city'] for loc in locations_data})
             vehicle_types = ['Economy', 'Compact', 'Sedan', 'SUV', 'Luxury']
             vehicles = read_vehicles()
             return render_template('search_vehicles.html', locations=locations, vehicle_types=vehicle_types, vehicles=vehicles)
         
         
         @app.route('/vehicle/<int:vehicle_id>')
         def vehicle_details(vehicle_id: int):
             vehicles = read_vehicles()
             vehicle = next((v for v in vehicles if v['vehicle_id'] == vehicle_id), None)
             if not vehicle:
                 return "Vehicle not found", 404
             # reviews data source not provided, empty list
             reviews: List[Dict[str, Union[str, int, float]]] = []
             return render_template('vehicle_details.html', vehicle=vehicle, reviews=reviews)
         
         
         @app.route('/book/<int:vehicle_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def booking(vehicle_id: int):
             vehicles = read_vehicles()
             vehicle = next((v for v in vehicles if v['vehicle_id'] == vehicle_id), None)
             if not vehicle or vehicle['status'] != 'Available':
                 return "Vehicle not available for booking", 400
             locations = read_locations()
             pickup_locations = [loc['city'] for loc in locations]
             dropoff_locations = pickup_locations.copy()
         
             booking_form: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None
             total_price: Optional[float] = None
             reservation_id: Optional[int] = None
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 pickup_location = request.form.get('pickup_location', '').strip()
                 dropoff_location = request.form.get('dropoff_location', '').strip()
                 pickup_date = request.form.get('pickup_date', '').strip()
                 dropoff_date = request.form.get('dropoff_date', '').strip()
         
                 if pickup_location not in pickup_locations or dropoff_location not in dropoff_locations:
                     return "Invalid pickup or dropoff location", 400
         
                 try:
                     pickup_dt = datetime.datetime.strptime(pickup_date, '%Y-%m-%d').date()
                     dropoff_dt = datetime.datetime.strptime(dropoff_date, '%Y-%m-%d').date()
                     if dropoff_dt < pickup_dt:
                         return "Dropoff date cannot be before pickup date", 400
                 except ValueError:
                     return "Invalid date format", 400
         
                 days = (dropoff_dt - pickup_dt).days + 1
                 total_price = round(days * vehicle['daily_rate'], 2)
         
                 booking_form = {
                     'pickup_location': pickup_location,
                     'dropoff_location': dropoff_location,
                     'pickup_date': pickup_date,
                     'dropoff_date': dropoff_date
                 }
         
                 # Create new rental
                 rental_id = get_next_rental_id()
                 # For simplicity, assign dummy customer_id 1
                 rental_entry = {
                     'rental_id': rental_id,
                     'vehicle_id': vehicle_id,
                     'customer_id': 1,
                     'pickup_date': pickup_date,
                     'dropoff_date': dropoff_date,
                     'pickup_location': pickup_location,
                     'dropoff_location': dropoff_location,
                     'total_price': total_price,
                     'status': 'Pending'
                 }
                 rentals = read_rentals()
                 rentals.append(rental_entry)
                 write_rentals(rentals)
         
                 # Create reservation linked to this rental with insurance_id=0 and empty special_requests
                 reservation_id = get_next_reservation_id()
                 reservations = read_reservations()
                 reservation_entry = {
                     'reservation_id': reservation_id,
                     'rental_id': rental_id,
                     'vehicle_id': vehicle_id,
                     'customer_id': 1,
                     'status': 'Pending',
                     'insurance_id': 0,
                     'special_requests': ''
                 }
                 reservations.append(reservation_entry)
                 write_reservations(reservations)
         
             return render_template('booking.html',
                                    pickup_locations=pickup_locations,
                                    dropoff_locations=dropoff_locations,
                                    booking_form=booking_form,
                                    total_price=total_price)
         
         
         @app.route('/insurance/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def insurance_options(reservation_id: int):
             insurance_plans = read_insurance()
             selected_insurance_id: Optional[int] = None
             insurance_details: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
         
             reservations = read_reservations()
             reservation = next((r for r in reservations if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id), None)
             if not reservation:
                 return "Reservation not found", 404
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 try:
                     selected_insurance_id = int(request.form.get('insurance_id', ''))
                 except (ValueError, TypeError):
                     return "Invalid insurance selection", 400
         
                 insurance_plan = next((i for i in insurance_plans if i['insurance_id'] == selected_insurance_id), None)
                 if not insurance_plan:
                     return "Insurance plan not found", 400
         
                 # Update reservation with selected insurance and status Confirmed
                 for r in reservations:
                     if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id:
                         r['insurance_id'] = selected_insurance_id
                         r['status'] = 'Confirmed'
                         break
                 write_reservations(reservations)
         
                 return redirect(url_for('rental_history'))
         
             if reservation['insurance_id'] != 0:
                 selected_insurance_id = reservation['insurance_id']
                 insurance_details = next((i for i in insurance_plans if i['insurance_id'] == selected_insurance_id), None)
             return render_template('insurance_options.html',
                                    insurance_plans=insurance_plans,
                                    selected_insurance_id=selected_insurance_id,
                                    insurance_details=insurance_details)
         
         
         @app.route('/rental-history')
         def rental_history():
             rentals = read_rentals()
             status_filter_options = ['All', 'Active', 'Completed', 'Cancelled']
             applied_status_filter = request.args.get('status_filter', 'All')
             if applied_status_filter != 'All':
                 rentals = [r for r in rentals if r['status'] == applied_status_filter]
             return render_template('rental_history.html',
                                    rentals=rentals,
                                    status_filter_options=status_filter_options,
                                    applied_status_filter=applied_status_filter)
         
         
         @app.route('/my-reservations')
         def reservations_page():
             reservations = read_reservations()
             return render_template('reservations.html', reservations=reservations)
         
         
         @app.route('/modify-reservation/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def modify_reservation(reservation_id: int):
             reservations = read_reservations()
             reservation = next((r for r in reservations if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id), None)
             if not reservation:
                 return "Reservation not found", 404
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # No modification schema specified; redirect back
                 return redirect(url_for('reservations_page'))
         
             return render_template('modify_reservation.html', reservation=reservation)
         
         
         @app.route('/cancel-reservation/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def cancel_reservation(reservation_id: int):
             reservations = read_reservations()
             found = False
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id:
                     r['status'] = 'Cancelled'
                     found = True
                     break
             if found:
                 write_reservations(reservations)
                 return redirect(url_for('reservations_page'))
             return "Reservation not found", 404
         
         
         @app.route('/special-requests', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def special_requests():
             reservations = read_reservations()
             form_data: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 try:
                     selected_reservation_id = int(request.form.get('select-reservation', '0'))
                 except ValueError:
                     return "Invalid reservation selection", 400
         
                 driver_assistance = 'driver-assistance-checkbox' in request.form
                 gps_option = 'gps-option-checkbox' in request.form
                 try:
                     child_seat_quantity = int(request.form.get('child-seat-quantity', '0'))
                     if child_seat_quantity < 0:
                         child_seat_quantity = 0
                 except ValueError:
                     child_seat_quantity = 0
                 special_notes = request.form.get('special-notes', '').strip()
         
                 updated = False
                 for r in reservations:
                     if r['reservation_id'] == selected_reservation_id:
                         details = []
                         if driver_assistance:
                             details.append('Driver assistance requested')
                         if gps_option:
                             details.append('GPS option requested')
                         if child_seat_quantity > 0:
                             details.append(f'Child seats: {child_seat_quantity}')
                         if special_notes:
                             details.append(f'Notes: {special_notes}')
                         r['special_requests'] = '; '.join(details) if details else ''
                         updated = True
                         form_data = {
                             'reservation_id': selected_reservation_id,
                             'driver_assistance': driver_assistance,
                             'gps_option': gps_option,
                             'child_seat_quantity': child_seat_quantity,
                             'special_notes': special_notes
                         }
                         break
                 if updated:
                     write_reservations(reservations)
         
             return render_template('special_requests.html', reservations=reservations, form_data=form_data)
         
         
         @app.route('/locations')
         def locations_page():
             locations = read_locations()
             hours_filter_options = ['24/7', 'Business Hours', 'Weekend']
             applied_hours_filter = request.args.get('hours_filter', '24/7')
             search_query = request.args.get('search_query', '').strip().lower()
         
             filtered_locations = locations
             if applied_hours_filter != '24/7':
                 if applied_hours_filter == 'Business Hours':
                     filtered_locations = [l for l in filtered_locations if l['hours'] == '09:00-18:00']
                 elif applied_hours_filter == 'Weekend':
                     # No weekend marker in data, so filter none
                     filtered_locations = []
         
             if search_query:
                 filtered_locations = [l for l in filtered_locations if search_query in l['city'].lower() or search_query in l['address'].lower()]
         
             return render_template('locations.html',
                                    locations=filtered_locations,
                                    hours_filter_options=hours_filter_options,
                                    applied_hours_filter=applied_hours_filter,
                                    search_query=search_query)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)

         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # --- Helper functions to read/write pipe-delimited files ---
         
         def read_vehicles() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             vehicles = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'vehicles.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 9:
                             continue
                         vehicle = {
                             'vehicle_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'make': parts[1],
                             'model': parts[2],
                             'vehicle_type': parts[3],
                             'daily_rate': float(parts[4]),
                             'seats': int(parts[5]),
                             'transmission': parts[6],
                             'fuel_type': parts[7],
                             'status': parts[8]
                         }
                         vehicles.append(vehicle)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return vehicles
         
         
         def read_customers() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             customers = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'customers.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         customer = {
                             'customer_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'name': parts[1],
                             'email': parts[2],
                             'phone': parts[3],
                             'driver_license': parts[4],
                             'license_expiry': parts[5]
                         }
                         customers.append(customer)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return customers
         
         
         def read_locations() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             locations = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'locations.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         location = {
                             'location_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'city': parts[1],
                             'address': parts[2],
                             'phone': parts[3],
                             'hours': parts[4],
                             'available_vehicles': int(parts[5])
                         }
                         locations.append(location)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return locations
         
         
         def read_rentals() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             rentals = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'rentals.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 9:
                             continue
                         rental = {
                             'rental_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'vehicle_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'customer_id': int(parts[2]),
                             'pickup_date': parts[3],
                             'dropoff_date': parts[4],
                             'pickup_location': parts[5],
                             'dropoff_location': parts[6],
                             'total_price': float(parts[7]),
                             'status': parts[8]
                         }
                         rentals.append(rental)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return rentals
         
         
         def write_rentals(rentals: List[Dict[str, Any]]):
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'rentals.txt'), 'w') as f:
                     for rental in rentals:
                         line = f"{rental['rental_id']}|{rental['vehicle_id']}|{rental['customer_id']}|{rental['pickup_date']}|{rental['dropoff_date']}|{rental['pickup_location']}|{rental['dropoff_location']}|{rental['total_price']}|{rental['status']}\n"
                         f.write(line)
             except Exception:
                 pass
         
         
         def read_insurance() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             insurances = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'insurance.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         # coverage_limit may be str or int
                         try:
                             coverage_limit = int(parts[4])
                         except ValueError:
                             coverage_limit = parts[4]
                         insurance = {
                             'insurance_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'plan_name': parts[1],
                             'description': parts[2],
                             'daily_cost': float(parts[3]),
                             'coverage_limit': coverage_limit,
                             'deductible': int(parts[5])
                         }
                         insurances.append(insurance)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return insurances
         
         
         def read_reservations() -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
             reservations = []
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reservations.txt'), 'r') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         line=line.strip()
                         if not line:
                             continue
                         parts = line.split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 7:
                             continue
                         reservation = {
                             'reservation_id': int(parts[0]),
                             'rental_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'vehicle_id': int(parts[2]),
                             'customer_id': int(parts[3]),
                             'status': parts[4],
                             'insurance_id': int(parts[5]),
                             'special_requests': parts[6]
                         }
                         reservations.append(reservation)
             except Exception:
                 pass
             return reservations
         
         
         def write_reservations(reservations: List[Dict[str, Any]]):
             try:
                 with open(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reservations.txt'), 'w') as f:
                     for r in reservations:
                         line = f"{r['reservation_id']}|{r['rental_id']}|{r['vehicle_id']}|{r['customer_id']}|{r['status']}|{r['insurance_id']}|{r['special_requests']}\n"
                         f.write(line)
             except Exception:
                 pass
         
         # --- Utility functions ---
         
         def get_next_reservation_id() -> int:
             reservations = read_reservations()
             if reservations:
                 return max(r['reservation_id'] for r in reservations) + 1
             else:
                 return 1
         
         def get_next_rental_id() -> int:
             rentals = read_rentals()
             if rentals:
                 return max(r['rental_id'] for r in rentals) + 1
             else:
                 return 1

         def dashboard():

             ]

         @app.route('/vehicle/<int:vehicle_id>')
         def vehicle_details(vehicle_id: int):

             if vehicle is None:
                 return "Vehicle not found", 404
             # There is no reviews.txt specified, reviews should be an empty list as no data source given
             reviews: List[Dict[str, Union[str, int, float]]] = []
             return render_template('vehicle_details.html', vehicle=vehicle, reviews=reviews)
         
         
         @app.route('/book/<int:vehicle_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def booking(vehicle_id: int):
             vehicles = read_vehicles()
             vehicle = next((v for v in vehicles if v['vehicle_id'] == vehicle_id), None)
             if vehicle is None or vehicle['status'] != 'Available':
                 return "Vehicle not available for booking", 400
         
             locations = read_locations()
             pickup_locations = [loc['city'] for loc in locations]
             dropoff_locations = pickup_locations.copy()
             booking_form: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None
             total_price: Optional[float] = None
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 pickup_location = request.form.get('pickup_location', '').strip()
                 dropoff_location = request.form.get('dropoff_location', '').strip()
                 pickup_date = request.form.get('pickup_date', '').strip()
                 dropoff_date = request.form.get('dropoff_date', '').strip()
         
                 # Validate pickup and dropoff locations
                 if pickup_location not in pickup_locations or dropoff_location not in dropoff_locations:
                     return "Invalid pickup or dropoff location", 400
         
                 # Validate dates format and logic
                 try:
                     pickup_dt = datetime.datetime.strptime(pickup_date, '%Y-%m-%d').date()
                     dropoff_dt = datetime.datetime.strptime(dropoff_date, '%Y-%m-%d').date()
                     if dropoff_dt < pickup_dt:
                         return "Dropoff date cannot be before pickup date", 400
                 except Exception:
                     return "Invalid date format", 400
         
                 # Calculate total price
                 days = (dropoff_dt - pickup_dt).days + 1
                 total_price = round(days * vehicle['daily_rate'], 2)
         
                 booking_form = {
                     'pickup_location': pickup_location,
                     'dropoff_location': dropoff_location,
                     'pickup_date': pickup_date,
                     'dropoff_date': dropoff_date
                 }
         
             return render_template('booking.html',
                                    pickup_locations=pickup_locations,
                                    dropoff_locations=dropoff_locations,
                                    booking_form=booking_form,
                                    total_price=total_price)
         
         
         @app.route('/insurance/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def insurance_options(reservation_id: int):
             insurance_plans = read_insurance()
             selected_insurance_id: Optional[int] = None
             insurance_details: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
         
             # Find reservation to ensure it exists
             reservations = read_reservations()
             reservation = next((r for r in reservations if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id), None)
             if reservation is None:
                 return "Reservation not found", 404
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 try:
                     selected_insurance_id = int(request.form.get('insurance_id', ''))
                 except (TypeError, ValueError):
                     return "Invalid insurance selection", 400
         
                 # Validate selected insurance id exists
                 insurance_details = next((i for i in insurance_plans if i['insurance_id'] == selected_insurance_id), None)
                 if insurance_details is None:
                     return "Selected insurance plan not found", 400
         
                 # Update reservation insurance_id
                 for r in reservations:
                     if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id:

                                    insurance_details=insurance_details)

         @app.route('/modify-reservation/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def modify_reservation(reservation_id:int):
             # Load reservation
             reservations = read_reservations()
             reservation = next((r for r in reservations if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id), None)
             if reservation is None:
                 return "Reservation not found", 404
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # No schema for modifications given, so cannot update fields

                 return redirect(url_for('reservations_page'))
         
             # For GET return reservation

         @app.route('/cancel-reservation/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def cancel_reservation(reservation_id: int):
             reservations = read_reservations()
             found = False
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id:
                     r['status'] = 'Cancelled'
                     found = True
                     break
             if found:
                 write_reservations(reservations)
                 # Redirect back to reservations page
                 return redirect(url_for('reservations_page'))
             return "Reservation not found", 404
         
         
         @app.route('/special-requests', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def special_requests():
             reservations = read_reservations()
             submitted_data: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # form fields (by IDs in spec): select-reservation, driver-assistance-checkbox, gps-option-checkbox, child-seat-quantity, special-notes
                 try:
                     selected_reservation_id = int(request.form.get('select-reservation', '0'))
                 except ValueError:
                     return "Invalid reservation selection", 400
         
                 driver_assistance = 'driver-assistance-checkbox' in request.form
                 gps_option = 'gps-option-checkbox' in request.form
                 try:
                     child_seat_quantity = int(request.form.get('child-seat-quantity', '0'))
                     if child_seat_quantity < 0:
                         child_seat_quantity = 0
                 except ValueError:
                     child_seat_quantity = 0
                 special_notes = request.form.get('special-notes', '').strip()
         
                 # Append special requests to reservation special_requests (concatenate strings?)
                 reservations_data = []
                 for r in reservations:
                     if r['reservation_id'] == selected_reservation_id:
                         details = []
                         if driver_assistance:
                             details.append('Driver assistance requested')
                         if gps_option:
                             details.append('GPS option requested')
                         if child_seat_quantity > 0:
                             details.append(f'Child seats: {child_seat_quantity}')
                         if special_notes:
                             details.append(f'Notes: {special_notes}')
         
                         special_string = '; '.join(details) if details else ''
                         r['special_requests'] = special_string
                         submitted_data = {
                             'reservation_id': selected_reservation_id,
                             'driver_assistance': driver_assistance,
                             'gps_option': gps_option,
                             'child_seat_quantity': child_seat_quantity,
                             'special_notes': special_notes
                         }
                     reservations_data.append(r)
         
                 write_reservations(reservations_data)
         
             return render_template('special_requests.html', reservations=reservations, submitted_data=submitted_data)
         
         
         @app.route('/locations')
         def locations_page():
             locations = read_locations()
             hours_filter_options = ['24/7', 'Business Hours', 'Weekend']
             applied_hours_filter = request.args.get('hours_filter', '24/7')
             search_query = request.args.get('search_query', '').strip().lower()
         
             filtered_locations = locations
         
             # Apply hours filter
             if applied_hours_filter != '24/7':
                 if applied_hours_filter == 'Business Hours':
                     # Filter locations with hours matching 09:00-18:00 exactly
                     filtered_locations = [loc for loc in filtered_locations if loc['hours'] == '09:00-18:00']
                 elif applied_hours_filter == 'Weekend':
                     # No clear spec for weekend filter; no special marker in data, so no filter or empty
                     filtered_locations = []
         
             # Apply search query by city or name
             if search_query:
                 filtered_locations = [loc for loc in filtered_locations if search_query in loc['city'].lower() or search_query in loc['address'].lower()]
         
             return render_template('locations.html',
                                    locations=filtered_locations,
                                    hours_filter_options=hours_filter_options,
                                    applied_hours_filter=applied_hours_filter,
                                    search_query=search_query)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)
